z1. asynchronous
1. synchronous (with a clock signal for synchronization)
2. synchronous microprogramable (operation defined by µprogram)
---
$Y^{t}=F(X^{t},X^{t-T_{1}},X^{t-T_{2}},\dots)$

More's machine
$Y^{t}=F_{1}(Q^{t})$               $Q^{t}$-Internal state of the machine in time
$Q^{t}=F_{2}(X^{t},Q^{t-T})$

Meoly's machine
$Y^{t}=F_{1}(Q^{t},X^{t})$

Bistable device (flip-flop, or basic latch)
$Q^{t}-Q$
$Q^{t-T}-q$

$Q=\overline{ \overline{ I+q }+r }=\overline{ \overline{ s+q } }·\overline{ r }=(s+q)·\overline{ r }$

r-reset

| --- | --- | ------------------------ |
| 00  | q   | store                    |
| 01  | 0   | reset                    |
| 10  | 1   | set                      |
| 11  | 0   | -not normally<br>allowed |

Excitation table

| q->Q | sr  |
| ---- | --- |

# Huffman's method of asynchronous circuits
1. Organise the design specifications as time chart with assigned states
2. Obtain a primitive flow map
3. Determine (pseudo-)equivalent states and eliminate redundancy in the primitive flow map
4. By using merger-diagram obtain the reduced flow map ( for Moore's or Meoly's machine)
5.  Encode the rows in the reduced flow map (avoiding critical races) and obtain composite K-map
6. Decompose the composite K-map and obtain functions for gates based or flip-flop based solution
---
## Example: design a sequencial circuit implementing the following timing chart

SOP static 1 hazard

IF you are using group composed of 1's then you don't need to eliminate hazard

for reset we consider 0s as 1s

TLDR: when using rslatch you can ignore hazard

set reset

| JK  | $Q^{n+1}$            |          |
| --- | -------------------- | -------- |
| 00  | $Q^{n}$              | storing  |
| 01  | 0                    | reseting |
| 10  | 1                    | seting   |
| 11  | $\overline{ Q^{n} }$ | toggling |


| $Q^{n}\to Q^{n+1}$ | JK  |
| ------------------ | --- |
| 00                 | 0-  |
| 01                 | 1-  |
| 11                 | -1  |
| 10                 | -0  |


|           | async | sync      |
| --------- | ----- | --------- |
| $Q^{t}$   | Q     | $Q^{n+1}$ |
| $Q^{t-T}$ | q     | $Q^{n}$   |
